In the Earth there is a wall with some dynamites to be hit and cylinder collectors to approach the concept of horizontal range. The parabolic movement is shown through a trail of smoke left by the projectile. In the Moon there is no explosions and smoke.\r\nAs the objective of this simulator is to demonstrate the phenomenon qualitatively, it does not provide any numerical output data, such as maximum height reached by the projectile or horizontal range of the trajectory.
